22/08/19, 5:32 pm - Ayush Khedia: Jo bhi interested hai, chale jana.
22/08/19, 5:34 pm - Ayush Khedia: *Thunderstrock Festival* is a rock/metal music festival which takes place in Ranchi, Jharkhand. The idea of Thunderstrock emerged back in the year 2008. The prominent bands and musicians of that time took the initiatives of the concert.

Thunderstrock is not just a concert, it's an idea to support and up-bring the rock bands and music lovers of Ranchi. Simultaneously, the idea is to donate the income generated from tickets and support someone who is truly engaged in the welfare of the society. *The festival today stands as the only Do-It-Yourself festival in Eastern India* which is completely funded by the organizers who initiate the event and the ticket sales. There is no sponsors for this festival which can bring any type of help or support. The festival is dedicated towards bringing independent and newly emerging live acts based in genres mostly metal and it's sub-genres. The income generated is hence donated to the charitable societies and non-governmental organizations.
22/08/19, 5:35 pm - Ayush Khedia: *Thunderstrock Festival 2019's* line-up includes,
- Atript from Jamshedpur, Jharkhand
- Bipolar Shadows from Gangtok, Sikkim
- Cross Affinity from Bhubaneswar, Odisha
- Reciprocal from Ranchi, Jharkhand
- Sparsh from Ranchi, Jharkhand

Our tickets are the cheapest music festival tickets you can find in India. *It is just Rs. 100 only* and will be available at the venue. The venue for Thunderstrock Festival 2019 is Ascot International School, Harmu By Pass Road, Kishoreganj, Ranchi.

22/09/19, 4:34 pm - Rishik Kumar: *MIXING AND MASTERING WORKSHOP - DHWANI*

Have you ever wondered why a singer's voice in a song sounds magical? Is it really that crisp, clear, accurate and flawless? Well, The answer is NO. It is the sound engineers who make their voice sound absolutely amazing. The singer sings the song in 2 hours and the sound engineers process the sound for 1-2 weeks to make sure the singer and the song sounds amazing. To know how it is done, fill the form and join the workshop. This is a Pre, Post and Live sound processing workshop organised by Dhwani - Music Club, BIT Mesra.  Please come with a notebook and pen.

*Venue -* Music Room
*Day -* Tue/Thu
*Timings -* In evening after Classes/Quiz

For Queries, Whatsapp - 8987400143, Rishik

Hum ko mili hai aaj
 Ye ghadiya naseeb se
 Je bhar ke dekh leejiye
 Hamako kareeb se
 Phir apke naseeb mein
 Ye raat ho na ho
 Phir is janaam mein
 Mulakat ho na ho
 
 Lag ja gale ki phir
 Ye hasin raat ho na ho
 
 Pas aiye ki ham nahin
 Ayenge baar baar
 Bahen gale mein daal ke
 Ham ro le zaar-zaar
 Ankhoon se phir ye
 Pyaar ki barsaat ho na ho
 Shayad phir is janam mein
 Mulakat ho na ho

01/01/20, 9:44 pm - Arpan Mitra: Hola amigos!!

We, the Indian Music Club, IIT BHU present the 3rd edition of Tarang, the online instrumental competition where you can flaunt your talent in front of the audience you've been craving for.

The rules of Tarang '20 are as follows:-
1)Videos should not be more than 4 minutes long.

2)The video will be judged based on the number of reactions on the video published under 'Tarang' on Instagram and Facebook page of the Indian Music Club, IIT (BHU).

3)We also have critics choice award wherein entries most loved by our jury (alumni and some of the most experienced members of the club), would be declared winners.

4)All instruments are permitted. Beatboxing is also permitted.

5)All genres are accepted.

6)Original compositions are welcome.

7)The entry can have at most one accompanying instrument, and /or a backing track.

8)Vocal accompaniment is not allowed.

9)The video should feature participants playing in real time.

10)Mixed tracks and/or Studio Recordings are not allowed

11)The entries can be mailed to indianmusicclub.iitbhu1@gmail.com
Alternatively , participants can message us their videos on our Facebook page.
Make sure you specify your name, institution and the name of the song/piece/original composition.

12)The decision as to whether or not the video is eligible to be uploaded rests with the organising team. Only one entry per person is allowed.

So, what are you waiting for? Record your entries and get a chance to win exciting prizes!!

And without any doubt, NAAD'20 was Dhwani's most successful and the biggest event till date. We all know why. Going for the credentials, firstly, we had 9 highly qualified and esteemed judges in the judges panel from all over India, and we all got a chance to sing along with them in the finale. Secondly apne club walo ko competitions me push karne ki zaroorat hi nahi padi, coz outside colleges aur schools se har competition me itna heavy participation. Then, a total cash prize of Rs 12000, goodies me 3 wireless headphones, 5 wired headphones, 10 wireless headphones, coupons by Chocolate room & Dosa plaza etc etc. And 9 SPONSORS.
